40 2021-04-06 eye movement disorder Approximately seven minutes after the patient received the Janssen COVID vaccine, he had called out ... Read more
Close
Approximately seven minutes after the patient received the Janssen COVID vaccine, he had called out to his wife/pharmacy technician at the pharmacy stating he did not feel well. His head had fallen back and his eyes were starting to roll back into his head. Patient had saliva starting to foam at the corner of his mouth and it appeared to be the onset of a mild seizure (per wife, patient has had seizure once before after a head injury) and he was turning very pale. Patient seemed to be unresponsive at that time - not answering to questions. At this point, one of the pharmacists ran to the clinic to get help and the other pharmacist administered an Epi-pen to patient's thigh. Patient immediately came around after the injection, looked up and began talking. Staff called 911 and patient was monitored by pharmacy and clinic staff. When the paramedics arrived, the patient was doing better and was able to ride home with his wife.

I had the worst headache of my life on 3/22 but assumed it was a migraine and treated it as such. On 3/23 while playing hockey, nearly immediately after starting, the headache returned even stronger than on 3/22 and forced me to stop playing as I could not concentrate or focus. The headache lasted for several days. The following morning I went to my standard physician who immediately sent me to the ER because he was concerned about a potential aneurysm. No cause was ever determined as the tests were inconclusive but it was suspected to potentially be a pinched nerve. However, I never had any pain in my neck or elsewhere besides the headache.

40 2021-04-19 thirst Unusual exhaustion within an hour of the vaccine. Had to go to bed and slept into the evening devel... Read more
Close
Unusual exhaustion within an hour of the vaccine. Had to go to bed and slept into the evening developing a fever of 103, severe thirst and chills. The fever lasted until 10:00 a.m. the following day, but weakness, thirst, chills and body aches continued for 3 more days intermittently. I would feel like I could finally exercise and then be too weak and tired to go back to routine. My appetite declined for 4 to 5 days as food didn't taste appealing. On Thursday, April 8, I announced to my mom in the morning that I finally felt like I was back at almost 100% and later in the afternoon felt nauseous, incredible pain in my chest and had dry heaves. I finally vomited some and was once again overcome by a fever of 101 and all I could do was sleep from severe exhaustion. I am against medication, but finally agreed to taking ibuprofen and tums. After sleeping into the next day around noon, I finally was able to eat some breakfast but the pain in my chest continued and I could rid it for another day. I intermittently had to sleep and gave up my exercise routine until my body has had time to recuperate. I have not fully recovered, but my appetite is picking up. I still require more sleep than normal.

40 2021-05-02 lacrimation increased Got injected, didn?t hurt much. Was told to wait 15 minutes in case of reaction. They walked away an... Read more
Close
Got injected, didn?t hurt much. Was told to wait 15 minutes in case of reaction. They walked away and left me sitting in a chair in a public space with everyone else who was waiting. I texted my wife to check in, when I started tearing up and crying for no real reason, then started feeling nauseous so I closed my eyes. Suddenly I felt like I had been given a shot of adrenaline out of nowhere so I?m just trying to figure out if it?s nerves or a physiological response to something. I?m trying to control my breathing but having a hard time breathing. Then the fever hit. The most intense flash of heat. I was hyperventilating. I couldn?t open my eyes or move or make a sound, I could just sit there struggling to breathe. My phone was in my hand and I couldn?t lift it. I just simply didn?t have the strength or energy to move. At some point I legit thought I was about to die. I managed to angle my wrist so I could check my heart rate with my watch. It was 47bpm. I was fading away but I made myself get control of my breathing and forced myself to take long deep slow breaths. It hurt, and I felt like passing out, but I kept doing it. Fever turned into chills and then I soaked through my jeans and T-shirt in under a minute. I was finally thinking clearly and breathing and getting oxygen. Everyone else near me was fine. Nobody checked on me the entire time including the 3 people who sat there and watched me suffer through this. I told the pharmacist about my reaction and asked if it was normal and didn?t receive any indication that I should be concerned, so I went home since I felt better. It wasn?t until my friend pointed out that this sounds like anaphylaxis that I thought I should report it. So here I am. Hopefully I?ll be okay.

Close
The next day I noticed tinnitus (high pitch mild ringing in both ears) . Therefore it has been a total of 7 days with ringing in both ears and it has not gone away. It has been constant, no pulses, no frequency changes, etc. Just constant high pitch ringing in both ears. Sometimes by inner ear feels funny, slightly tingle feeling that is related to the tinnitus. The tinnitus is most noticeable in quiet settings, sleeping, reading, watching TV, I do not noticed it as much in office environments, listening to music, walking outside. I have experienced tinnitus in the past after loud music band or rock concert but do not attend live loud music often and try to avoid it because it hurts my ears. I do not have any known hearing problem, I try to protect my ears and use hearing protection often to avoid damage. When I cut my lawn I wear hearing protection, when I am working on shop floor I wear hearing protection. I am thinking the vaccine is related somehow. I never had COVID-19 in past. I use to be able to be in quiet settings and not have any tinnitus before vaccine.

41 2021-04-11 taste impairment FEVER OF 102-107F; SHAKINESS; VOMITING; SENSATION OF COLD; CHILLS AND SHIVERING; HALLUCINATIONS; WEI... Read more

FEVER OF 102-107F; SHAKINESS; VOMITING; SENSATION OF COLD; CHILLS AND SHIVERING; HALLUCINATIONS; WEIRD TASTE IN MOUTH; This spontaneous report received from a patient concerned male. The patient's height, and weight were not reported. The patient's concurrent conditions included seasonal allergies, acid reflux, and heat burn. The patient received covid-19 vaccine ad26.cov2.s (suspension for injection, route of admin not reported, batch number: 1808980, expiry: UNKNOWN) dose was not reported, administered on 01-APR-2021 around 1-1:20 pm to the left arm for prophylactic vaccination. Concomitant medications include blood thinners, medication for heart burn and acid reflux. Patient did not take his medicines on the day of his vaccination and few days after the vaccination. On 01-APR-2021 23:00, the patient experienced chills and shivering, fever of 102-107F, sensation of cold, vomiting and shakiness. Patient had not contacted his MD and had not taken any medications to manage those symptoms. At the time of calling (on the day of reporting), patient was feeling better but was having weird taste in mouth. On the same night of the vaccination (01-APR-2021), patient started experiencing hallucinations. The person who took this report on call recommended patient seeing his doctor regarding hallucinations. There were no hallucinations at the time of reporting. Laboratory data included: Body temperature (NR: not provided) 102-107 F. The action taken with covid-19 vaccine ad26.cov2.s was not applicable. The patient recovered from hallucinations, shakiness, sensation of cold, chills and shivering, and fever of 102-107f on APR-2021, had not recovered from weird taste in mouth, and the outcome of vomiting was not reported. This report was serious (Other Medically Important Condition).; Sender's Comments: V0: 20210406953-COVID-19 VACCINE AD26.COV2.S-hallucination. This event is considered unassessable. The event has a compatible/suggestive temporal relationship, is unlabeled, and has unknown scientific plausibility. There is no information on any other factors potentially associated with the event. 2021040695300-COVID-19 VACCINE AD26.COV2.S-fever. This event is labeled per RSI and is therefore considered potentially related.

Doctor, after his examination and consulting with another neurologist, said that he suspected Cranial nerve Palsy and possible Myasthenia Gravis. doctor suggested that if the patient wanted answers right away, then check into the Emergency Room (ER). The patient was waiting for a call back from the neurologists for a follow-up appointment and further treatment, if any. 47 2021-04-20 toothache The vaccination uncovered an ongoing, hitherto silent infection: after a few days, my teeth started ... Read more
Close
The vaccination uncovered an ongoing, hitherto silent infection: after a few days, my teeth started hurting, with the pain intensity increasing over two days to the point where I had to see a dentist. It turned out I had a molar that was infected and needed a root canal. The immune response from the vaccine probably caused my body to react to the tooth infection as well. I normally wouldn't put the two things together, but I had a very similar reaction a few days after my flu vaccine back in October: sensitive teeth, wandering pain in different parts of my head, neck, and shoulder area. At that time, the dentist didn't find anything (although we now know it was probably the start of that same tooth becoming infected and dying), and antibiotics took care of it. The root canal specialist I saw, the dr, said she is seeing a number of similar cases in her patients, where vaccinations bring out undetected problems. I actually consider that a good thing - I wouldn't want to have a rotting tooth that goes unnoticed for a while.

I had previously had COVID during the first week of January 2021 and recovered. During that time, I had lost about 80% of my sense of smell which I still have not regained. But at time, I never has any loss of taste. However, immediately after receiving the vaccination I noticed an altered sense of taste. I would describe it as almost all of my sense of taste is gone but actually everything I eat has a rancid taste. Some foods cause the bad taste more than others. Some foods I used to love now bring out the worst after taste such as peanut butter. The more bland the food usually results in less "bad" taste. But overall I can't really taste the actual taste of any food. And to make it worse, before when I couldn?t smell, it was bearable, but now most of the same foods that taste bad also have the same rancid odor I smell also. So to summarize, I now can?t really taste or smell anything except for the rancid taste and odor the food has. It is amazingly challenging as people don?t understand when I describe it to them that almost all food smells and tastes bad since that isn?t just loss of taste. As of today, it has now been over 3 weeks since my vaccination and I don't see any improvement yet. I did recently (about 2 week ago) have full lab work done as part of an annual checkup and all results came back normal. So now I have reduced smell from COVID and loss of taste from the vaccine. I don?t see any other explanation than that the vaccine caused this new phenomenon. It could has something to do with the fact that I previously had COVID. I am hesitant to even go to the doctor since I am certain they will have no idea what to do.

This only lasted no more than 10-30 minutes, and this resolved on its own as well. He continues to have intermittent headaches, again otherwise nonspecific with pounding quality however the intensity is improved. Humidifier regarding the Johnson & Johnson vaccine to report any side effects, for which she had notified his primary care doctor who then decided to proceed with MRI of the brain to evaluate for possible etiology. The MRI was done with and without contrast at facility on 5/4/2021, for which there was concern for possible left temporal posterior stroke, and if there was any concern for venous thrombosis, further imaging was necessary. He was then recommended to go to the emergency room for evaluation. He otherwise is in his regular state of health. He denies any recent fever or chills or cough, no chest pain or shortness of breath, nausea, vomiting, abdominal pain. No changes in bowel or bladder habits.
